Function prototypes are declared in gcc/targhooks.h:305.\\n\\n4. **Generic Implementation (gcc/explow.cc, gcc/explow.h)**: The core stack clash protection logic resides in gcc/explow.cc:\\n\\n   a. **allocate_dynamic_stack_space (gcc/explow.cc:1443+)**: High-level function that allocates dynamic stack space. When flag_stack_clash_protection is set, it calls anti_adjust_stack_and_probe_stack_clash instead of the standard anti_adjust_stack_and_probe (lines 1645-1646).\\n\\n   b. **anti_adjust_stack_and_probe_stack_clash (gcc/explow.cc:2072-2142)**: Implements the stack clash protection mechanism for dynamic allocations. This function:\\n      - Ensures the size is in Pmode (line 2075-2076)\\n      - Calls compute_stack_clash_protection_loop_data to calculate probe parameters (line 2082-2083)\\n      - Retrieves target-specific probe range via targetm.stack_clash_protection_alloca_probe_range() (line 2086)\\n      - For small allocations (≤4*probe_interval), emits inline probes (line 2098-2108)\\n      - For larger allocations, emits a probing loop using emit_stack_clash_protection_probe_loop_start/end\\n\\n   c. **compute_stack_clash_protection_loop_data (gcc/explow.cc:1955-2004)**: Calculates loop parameters:\\n      - Extracts probe_interval from param_stack_clash_protection_probe_interval (line 1961-1962)\\n      - Rounds the allocation size down to probe_interval boundary (line 1963-1964)\\n      - Computes the final stack pointer value (last_addr) (line 1969-1972)\\n      - Calculates residual bytes not covered by the loop (line 1976)\\n\\n   d. **emit_stack_clash_protection_probe_loop_start (gcc/explow.cc:2014+)**: Emits RTL instructions for loop initialization, including loop label and initial comparison.\\n\\n   e. **emit_stack_clash_protection_probe_loop_end (gcc/explow.cc:2036+)**: Emits RTL instructions for the loop body and termination logic.\\n\\n5. **x86_64 Integration (gcc/config/i386/i386.cc)**: While the generic mechanism in gcc/explow.cc handles most of the work, gcc/config/i386/i386.cc provides x86-specific prologue/epilogue generation and frame management. This implementation prevents this by:\\n1. Probing at regular intervals (typically 4KB on x86)\\n2. Never skipping probes even for small allocations\\n3. This implementation prevents this by:\\n1. Probing at regular intervals (typically 4KB on x86)\\n2. Never skipping probes even for small allocations\\n3.
